#          =使用 kubelet做Tomcat容器的部署=   

```markdown
启动 etcd, docker, kube-apiserver, kube-controller-manager,kube-scheduler
    kube-proxy, kubelet 


#部署一个tomcat，写配置文件，控制（配置）tomcat容器（docker镜像创建的）
#创建一个木哭k8s在里面写配置文件 mytomcat.rc.yaml 和 mytomcat.svc.yaml
yaml文件的书写格式需要注意
```

## ======= mytomcat.rc.yaml属于创建副本文件 ========

```markdown
# mytomcat.rc.yaml
#-----------------------------------------------------
apiVersion: v1
kind: ReplicationController
metadata:
 name: mytomcat
spec:
 replicas: 2
 selector:
  app: mytomcat
 template:
  metadata:
   labels:
   app: mytomcat
  spec:
   containers:
   - name: mytomcat
     image: tomcat7-jre
     ports:
     - containerPort: 8080
#-----------------------------------------------------
```

## =mytomcat.svc.yaml 属于tomcat容器的的配置:容器叫POD=

```markdown
# mytomcat.svc.yaml
#-----------------------------------------------------
apiVersion : v1
kind: Service
metadata:
 name: mytomcat
spec:
 type: NodePort
 ports:
  - port: 8080
  nodePort: 30001
 selector:
  app: mytomcat
#-----------------------------------------------------
```

```markdown
# 使用 kubernete的组件  keubectl 执行tomcat文件
# kubectl create -f mytomcat.rc.yaml
# kubectl create -f mytomcat.svc.yaml
# 使用 kubectl get pods 没有获得相关的数据
```

# 解决方案1：其实就是把 把镜像 下载下来到本地了

```markdown
# 创建容器时添加参数 --restart=always 后，当 docker 重启时，容器自动启动

### 安装的机器节点是的 227 上
关闭防火墙
# yum install -y etcd kubernetes
# 开启
systemctl start etcd
systemctl status etcd
systemctl start docker
systemctl status docker
systemctl start kube-apiserver                      (我的没启动成功)
systemctl status kube-apiserver 
systemctl start kube-controller-manager
systemctl status kube-controller-manager
systemctl start kube-scheduler
systemctl status kube-scheduler
systemctl start kubelet
systemctl status kubelet
systemctl start kube-proxy
systemctl status kube-proxy
# 关闭
systemctl stop etcd
systemctl stop docker
systemctl stop apiserver
systemctl stop kube-scheduler
systemctl stop kube-schedualer
systemctl stop kubelet
systemctl stop kube-proxy

# 卸载
yum remove -y kubelet kubeadm kubectl
 
kubeadm reset -f
modprobe -r ipip
lsmod
rm -rf ~/.kube/
rm -rf /etc/kubernetes/
rm -rf /etc/systemd/system/kubelet.service.d
rm -rf /etc/systemd/system/kubelet.service
rm -rf /usr/bin/kube*
rm -rf /etc/cni
rm -rf /opt/cni
rm -rf /var/lib/etcd
rm -rf /var/etcd
```

# K8s集群安装

```markdown
# 这种安装方式可以了解更多的细节 主要是为了学习，可以更简yum直接安装K8s 搭建集群
下载二进制包： https://github.com/kubernetes/
官网：https://kubernetes.io/

# 安装docker. 已经存在yum源 包括了国内的阿里云的源 在 /etc/yum.repo.d/docker-ce
# yum install docker-ce

# 下载etcd https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/releases
直接安装包传输的其他节点 228， 229
# scp -r etcd-v3.5.5-linux-arm64 root@172.16.136.228:/usr/local/software/k8s/
# scp -r etcd-v3.5.5-linux-arm64 root@172.16.136.229:/usr/local/software/k8s/
拷贝安装包种的 etcd, etcdctl到 /etc/bin目录下
# cp etcd /usr/bin/
# cp etcdctl /usr/bin/
# 在/etc/sysconfig/可执行目录并创建服务etcd.service
# vim /usr/lib/systemd/system/etcd.service
etcd.service文件中写入如下内容
#------------------------------------------------
[unit]
Description=Etcd Server
After=network.target
[Service]
Type=simple
EnvirimentFile=-/etc/etcd/etcd.conf
WorkingDirectory=/var/lib/etcd/
ExecStart=/usr/bin/etcd
Restart=on-failure
[install]
WantedBy=mutil-user.target
#------------------------------------------------
# 上面的描述 需要在/var/lib/etcd/创建此目录  mkdir
mkdir /var/lib/etcd



# 启动与测试edct服务
# systemctl daemon-reload
# systemctl start etcd.service
# systemctl enable etcd.service
# mkdir -p /var/lib/etcd.service
# etcdctl cluster-health


# 下载 Kubernets-server 的二进制包 
https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/CHANGELOG/CHANGELOG-1.25.md#server-binaries
```

```markdown
# cp kube-apiserver kube-scheduler kube-controller-manager kubectl /usr/bin/
#  cp 过去相当于已经安装完成了，
下面就是和上面一样写配置信息文件

# 创建文件服务 vim /usr/lib/systemd/system/kube-apiserver.service
写入文件：
#---------------------------------------------------
[Unit]
Description=Kubernetes API Server
Documentation=https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes
After=etcd.service
Wants=etcd.service
[Service]
EnviromentFile=/etc/kubernetes/apiserver
ExecStart=/usr/bin/kube-apiserver $KUBE_API_ARGS
Restart=on-failure
Type=notify
[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
#---------------------------------------------------
创建配置文件
目录：
# mkdir /etc/kubernetes
# vi /etc/kubernetes/apiserver
写入： 
# KUBE_API_ARGS="--storage-backend --etcd3 --etcd-servers=http://127.0.0.1:2379 --insecure-bind-address=0.0.0.0 --insecure-port=8080 --service-cluster-ip-range=172.16.0.0/16 --service-node-port-range=1-65535 --admission-control=NamespaceLifecycle,NamespaceExists,LimitRange,SecurityContextDeny,ServiceAccount,DefaultStorageClass,ResourceQuota --logtostderr=true --log-dir=/var/log/kubernetes --v=2"
```

```markdown
创建文件
# vim /usr/lib/systemd/system/kube-controller-manager.service
#---------------------------------------------------------------
[Unit]
Description=Kubernetes api Server
Documentation=https://github.com/GoogleCloudPlatform/kubernetes
After=kube-apiserver.service
Requrires=kube-apiserver.service
[Service]
EnviromentFile=/etc/kubernetes/controller-manager
ExecStart=/usr/bin/kube-controller-manager $KUBE-CONTROLLER-MANAGER_ARGS
Restart=on-failure
LimitNOFILE=65535
[Install]
WantedBy=mutil-user.target
#---------------------------------------------------------------
```

```markdown
#---------------------------------------------------

[Unit]
Description=Kubernetes Scheduler
Documentation=https://github.com/GoogleCloudPlatform/kubernetes
After=kube-apiserver.service
Requrires=kube-apiserver.service

[Service]
EnviromentFile=/etc/kubernetes/controller-manager
ExecStart=/usr/bin/kube-scheduler $KUBE-SCHEDULER_ARGS
Restart=on-failure
LimitNOFILE=65535

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

#--------------------------------------------------
```

# 如果还是找不到， 那就可能是网络问题， 上面有解决网络问题的方案

## ====== 部署 Nginx 镜像 ===============在集群中

```markdown
# cd /usr/lolca/k8s下， 没有就创建，
# 创建 Nginx 的配置文件  nginx-rc.yaml文件 ==============> 创建 Nginx 镜像
```

```markdown
## 然后通过 kubectl get pods 查看，如果没找到pod,
# 没找到的原因是 镜像拉取有问题, 默认情况下啊他是从 gc.io仓库区拉取 


# 这个时候我们需要去搭建私有仓库去拉去  
docker pull registry
拉取完成后需要打上标签，然后上传到 私有仓库
修改 （在 该node节点上搭建私有仓库）
```
